services, virtualServices,\n    57→// and destinationRules that are accessible to a given\n    58→// sidecar. Precomputing the list of services, virtual services, dest rules\n    59→// for a sidecar improves performance as we no longer need to compute this\n    60→// list for every sidecar. We simply have to match a sidecar to a\n    61→// SidecarScope. Note that this is not the same as public/private scoped\n    62→// services. The list of services seen by every sidecar scope (namespace\n    63→// wide or per workload) depends on the imports, the listeners, and other\n    64→// settings.\n    65→//\n    66→// Every proxy workload of SidecarProxy type will always map to a\n    67→// SidecarScope object. 407→\t\tout.servicesByHostname[s.Hostname] = s\n   408→\t\tif drList := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); drList != nil {\n   409→\t\t\tout.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = drList\n 428→\t}\n   429→\n   430→\treturn out\n   431→}\n   432→\n   433→func convertIstioListenerToWrapper(ps *PushContext, configNamespace string,\n   434→\tistioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener) the catch all listener\n   465→func (sc *SidecarScope) GetEgressListenerForRDS(port int, bind string) *IstioEgressListenerWrapper {\n   466→\tif sc == nil {\n   467→\t\treturn nil\n   468→\t}\n   469→\n   470→\tfor _, e := range sc.EgressListeners {\n   471→\t\t// We hit a catchall listener. 477→\t\t// Check if the ports match\n   478→\t\t// for unix domain sockets (i.e. port == 0), check if the bind is equal to the routeName\n   479→\t\tif int(e.IstioListener.Port.Number) == port {\n   480→\t\t\tif port == 0 { // unix domain socket\n   481→\t\t\t\tif e.IstioListener.Bind == bind {\n   482→\t\t\t\t\treturn e\n   483→\t\t\t\t}\n   484→\t\t\t\t// no match.. continue searching\n   485→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   486→\t\t\t}\n   487→\t\t\t// this is a non-zero port match\n   488→\t\t\treturn e\n   489→\t\t}\n   490→\t}\n   491→\n   492→\t// This should never be reached unless user explicitly set an empty array for egress\n   493→\t// listeners which we actually forbid\n   494→\treturn nil\n   495→}\n   496→\n   497→// HasIngressListener returns if the sidecar scope has ingress *SidecarScope) DestinationRule(direction TrafficDirection, proxy *Proxy, svc host.Name) *config.Config {\n   559→\tdestinationRules := sc.destinationRules[svc]\n   560→\tvar catchAllDr *config.Config\n   561→\tfor _, destRule := range destinationRules {\n   562→\t\tdestinationRule := destRule.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n   563→\t\tif destinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == destRule.Namespace &&\n   570→\t\t\tdestinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && direction == TrafficDirectionOutbound {\n   571→\t\t\tworkloadLabels := labels.Collection{proxy.Metadata.Labels}\n portion of the Sidecar config.\n   592→// Note that the returned service could be trimmed.\n   593→func (ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) selectServices(services []*Service, configNamespace string, hosts map[string][]host.Name) []*Service {\n   594→\timportedServices := make([]*Service, 0)\n   595→\twildcardHosts, wnsFound := hosts[wildcardNamespace]\n   596→\tfor _, s := range services {\n   597→\t\tconfigNamespace := s.Attributes.Namespace\n   598→\n   599→\t\t// Check if there is an explicit import of form ns/* or ns/host\n   600→\t\tif importedHosts, nsFound := hosts[configNamespace]; // Check if there is an import of form */host or */*\n   605→\t\t\tif svc := matchingService(wildcardHosts, s, ilw); svc != nil {\n   606→\t\t\t\timportedServices = append(importedServices, svc)\n   607→\t\t\t}\n   608→\t\t}\n   609→\t}\n   610→\n   611→\tvalidServices := make(map[host.Name]string)\n   612→\tfor _, svc := range importedServices {\n   613→\t\t_, f := validServices[svc.Hostname]\n 619→\t\t}\n   620→\t}\n   621→\n   622→\tfilteredServices := make([]*Service, 0)\n   623→\t// Filter down to just instances in scope for the service\n   624→\tfor _, svc := range importedServices {\n 630→}\n   631→\n   632→// Return the original service or a trimmed service which has a subset of the ports in original service.\n   633→func matchingService(importedHosts []host.Name, service *Service, ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) *Service {\n   634→\tmatchPort := needsPortMatch(ilw)\n   635→\tfor _, importedHost := range importedHosts {\n   636→\t\t// Check if the hostnames match per 641→\t\t\treturn service\n   642→\t\t}\n   643→\t}\n   644→\treturn nil\n   645→}\n   646→\n   647→// serviceMatchingListenerPort constructs service with listener port.\n   648→func 657→}\n   658→\n   659→func needsPortMatch(ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) bool {\n   660→\t// If a listener is defined with a port, we should match services with port except in the following case.\n   661→\t//  - If Port's protocol is proxy protocol(HTTP_PROXY) in which case the egress listener is used as generic egress http proxy.\n   662→\treturn ilw.IstioListener != nil && Sidecar resource with some\n// preprocessed data to determine the list of services, virtualServices,\n// and destinationRules that are accessible to a given\n// sidecar. Precomputing the list of services, virtual services, dest rules\n// for a sidecar improves performance as we no longer need to compute this\n// list for every sidecar. We simply have to match a sidecar to a\n// SidecarScope. Note that this is not the same as public/private scoped\n// services. The list of services seen by every sidecar scope (namespace\n// wide or per workload) depends on the imports, the listeners, and other\n// settings.\n//\n// Every proxy workload of SidecarProxy type will always map to a\n// SidecarScope object. If the proxy's namespace does not have a user\n// specified Sidecar CRD, we will construct one that has a catch all egress\n// listener that imports every public service/virtualService in the mesh.\ntype SidecarScope struct {\n\tName string\n\t// This is the namespace where the sidecar takes effect,\n\t// maybe different from the ns where sidecar resides if sidecar is in root ns.\n\tNamespace string\n\t// The crd itself. Can be nil if we are constructing the default\n\t// sidecar scope\n\tSidecar *networking.Sidecar\n\n\t// Version this sidecar was computed for\n\tVersion string\n\n\t// Set of egress listeners, and their associated services.  A sidecar\n\t// scope should have either ingress/egress listeners or both.  For\n\t// every proxy workload that maps to a sidecar API object (or the\n\t// default object), we will go through every egress listener in the\n\t// object and process the Envoy listener or RDS based on the imported\n\t// services/virtual services in that listener.\n\tEgressListeners []*IstioEgressListenerWrapper\n\n\t// Union of services imported across all egress listeners for use by CDS code.\n\tservices           []*Service\n\tservicesByHostname map[host.Name]*Service\n\n\t// Destination rules imported across all egress listeners. This\n\t// contains the computed set based on public/private destination rules\n\t// as well as the inherited ones, in addition to the wildcard matches\n\t// such as *.com applying to foo.bar.com. Each hostname in this map\n\t// corresponds to a service in the services array above. When computing\n\t// CDS, we simply have to find the matching service and return the\n\t// destination rule.\n\tdestinationRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config\n\t// OutboundTrafficPolicy defines the outbound traffic policy for this sidecar.\n\t// If OutboundTrafficPolicy is ALLOW_ANY traffic to unknown destinations will\n\t// be forwarded.\n\tOutboundTrafficPolicy *networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy\n\n\t// Set of known configs this sidecar depends on.\n\t// This field will be used to determine the config/resource scope\n\t// which means which config changes will affect the proxies within this scope.\n\tconfigDependencies map[uint64]struct{}\n\n\t// The namespace to treat as the administrative root namespace for\n\t// Istio configuration.\n\t//\n\t// Changes to Sidecar resources in this namespace will trigger a push.\n\tRootNamespace string\n}\n\n// MarshalJSON implements json.Marshaller\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error) {\n\t// Json cannot expose unexported fields, so copy the ones we want here\n\treturn json.MarshalIndent(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\"version\":               sc.Version,\n\t\t\"rootNamespace\":         sc.RootNamespace,\n\t\t\"name\":                  sc.Name,\n\t\t\"namespace\":             sc.Namespace,\n\t\t\"outboundTrafficPolicy\": sc.OutboundTrafficPolicy,\n\t\t\"services\":              sc.services,\n\t\t\"sidecar\":               sc.Sidecar,\n\t\t\"destinationRules\":      sc.destinationRules,\n\t}, \"\", \"  \")\n}\n\n// IstioEgressListenerWrapper is a wrapper for\n// networking.IstioEgressListener object. The wrapper provides performance\n// optimizations as it allows us to precompute and store the list of\n// services/virtualServices that apply to this listener.\ntype IstioEgressListenerWrapper struct {\n\t// The actual IstioEgressListener api object from the Config. It can be\n\t// nil if this is for the default sidecar scope.\n\tIstioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener\n\n\t// List of services imported by this egress listener above.\n\t// This will be used by LDS and RDS code when\n\t// building the set of virtual hosts or the tcp filterchain matches for\n\t// a given listener port. Two listeners, on user specified ports or\n\t// unix domain sockets could have completely different sets of\n\t// services. So a global list of services per sidecar scope will be\n\t// incorrect. Hence the per listener set of services.\n\tservices []*Service\n\n\t// List of virtual services imported by this egress listener above.\n\t// As with per listener services, this\n\t// will be used by RDS code to compute the virtual host configs for\n\t// http listeners, as well as by TCP/TLS filter code to compute the\n\t// service routing configs and the filter chain matches. We need a\n\t// virtualService set per listener and not one per sidecarScope because\n\t// each listener imports an independent set of virtual services.\n\t// Listener 1 could import a public virtual service for serviceA from\n\t// namespace A that has some path rewrite, while listener2 could import\n\t// a private virtual service for serviceA from the local namespace,\n\t// with a different path rewrite or no path rewrites.\n\tvirtualServices []config.Config\n\n\tlistenerHosts map[string][]host.Name\n}\n\nconst defaultSidecar = \"default-sidecar\"\n\n// DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace is a sidecar scope object with a default catch all egress listener\n// that matches the default Istio behavior: a sidecar has listeners for all services in the mesh\n// We use this scope when the user has not set any sidecar Config for a given config namespace.\nfunc DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps *PushContext, configNamespace string) *SidecarScope {\n\tdefaultEgressListener := {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01MKX4faSBzWomgd9rE8BzRe","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01666ubGTVq4orUUVofbRxRS","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/logs/agent/investigation.md","content":"# Investigation Report\n\n## Summary\n\nWhen multiple DestinationRules are created for the same host, the `mergeDestinationRule()` function in `pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go` merges their specifications (subsets, traffic policies) into a single consolidated config while discarding the metadata identity of the contributing DRs. Consequently, only the first DR's ConfigKey is registered in the proxy's `SidecarScope.configDependencies`. When a contributing DR that was not preserved in the consolidated config is updated, the update event does not match any registered dependency, causing `DependsOnConfig()` to return false and the proxy push to be incorrectly skipped, leaving the Envoy sidecar with stale configuration.\n\n## Root Cause\n\n**File:** `pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go` (merging logic)\n**Function:** `mergeDestinationRule()` (lines 38-109)\n**Mechanism:** Metadata loss during consolidation\n\nWhen multiple DestinationRules target the same FQDN host:\n\n1. **First DR arrives** → added to `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` (line 107)\n2. **Second DR arrives** → merges with first:\n   - Deep copies the first DR (line 65)\n   - Merges subsets and traffic policies from second DR into the copy (lines 77-93)\n   - Updates `p.destRules[resolvedHost][0]` with the merged copy (line 66)\n   - Does **not** add the second DR as a separate entry (line 101-104: `addRuleToProcessedDestRules` is false, so the second DR is discarded)\n\n**Result:** `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` now contains only one config.Config object (the first DR, with merged specs). The second DR's identity (Name, Namespace) is permanently lost.\n\n## Evidence\n\n### 1. Merging Logic (destination_rule.go:38-109)\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig config.Config, ...) {\n    // ...line 41: If a DR already exists for this host...\n    if mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n        // ...line 65-66: Deep copy the FIRST DR, modify it in-place\n        copied := mdr.DeepCopy()\n        p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied\n\n        // ...line 77-87: Add subsets from the NEW DR to the copied FIRST DR\n        for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n            mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n        }\n\n        // ...line 91-92: Add traffic policy from NEW DR if FIRST DR doesn't have one\n        if mergedRule.TrafficPolicy == nil && rule.TrafficPolicy != nil {\n            mergedRule.TrafficPolicy = rule.TrafficPolicy\n        }\n    }\n    // ...line 101-104: If addRuleToProcessedDestRules is false, do NOT add the new DR separately\n    if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {\n        p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Key Issue:** The `destRuleConfig` (second DR) is never added to `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` when `addRuleToProcessedDestRules` is false. Its specs are merged into a copy of the first DR, but its metadata (Name, Namespace from `destRuleConfig.Name` and `destRuleConfig.Namespace`) is lost forever.\n\n### 2. Dependency Tracking in SidecarScope (sidecar.go:219-227, 410-416)\n\n**DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace (lines 219-227):**\n```go\nfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,           // Only uses the config's Name field\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace,       // Only uses the config's Namespace field\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**ConvertToSidecarScope (lines 410-416):**\n```go\nfor _, dr := range drList {\n    out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n        Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n        Name:      dr.Name,               // Only uses the config's Name field\n        Namespace: dr.Namespace,           // Only uses the config's Namespace field\n    })\n}\n```\n\n**Problem:** Both iterate over `out.destinationRules` (which comes from `ps.destinationRule()`), which returns the consolidated list from `p.destRules[hostname]`. Since only the first DR is in this list, only its ConfigKey is registered. The second DR's ConfigKey is never added to `configDependencies`.\n\n### 3. xDS Push Filter (proxy_dependencies.go:60-74)\n\n```go\nfunc checkProxyDependencies(proxy *model.Proxy, config model.ConfigKey) bool {\n    switch proxy.Type {\n    case model.SidecarProxy:\n        if proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {  // Line 64\n            return true\n        } else if proxy.PrevSidecarScope != nil && proxy.PrevSidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n    return false\n}\n```\n\n**DependsOnConfig (sidecar.go:523-540):**\n```go\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) DependsOnConfig(config ConfigKey) bool {\n    // ... check for cluster-scoped configs ...\n\n    // Line 538: Check if this config's hash is in registered dependencies\n    _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n    return exists\n}\n```\n\n**Failure:** When an update event for the second DR (reviews-subsets) arrives, it creates a ConfigKey with Name=\"reviews-subsets\" and Namespace=\"default\". The hash of this key is looked up in `configDependencies`. Since only the first DR's key is registered, the lookup fails and `DependsOnConfig()` returns false. The proxy is not pushed.\n\n### 4. Config Update Event Handler (bootstrap/server.go:881-904)\n\n```go\nconfigHandler := func(prev config.Config, curr config.Config, event model.Event) {\n    pushReq := &model.PushRequest{\n        Full: true,\n        ConfigsUpdated: map[model.ConfigKey]struct{}{{\n            Kind:      curr.GroupVersionKind,       // DestinationRule\n            Name:      curr.Name,                   // reviews-subsets (when updated)\n            Namespace: curr.Namespace,               // default\n        }: {}},\n        Reason: []model.TriggerReason{model.ConfigUpdate},\n    }\n    s.XDSServer.ConfigUpdate(pushReq)\n}\n```\n\n**Result:** When `reviews-subsets` is updated, the event handler creates a PushRequest with ConfigKey{Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\"}. However, the proxy's `SidecarScope.configDependencies` only contains the hash of ConfigKey{Name: \"reviews-traffic-policy\", Namespace: \"default\"}. The push filtering rejects the update as not affecting this proxy.\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go**\n   - `mergeDestinationRule()` - Merges multiple DRs but discards metadata identity\n\n2. **pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go**\n   - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` - Registers only DRs present in consolidated list\n   - `ConvertToSidecarScope()` - Same limitation\n   - `AddConfigDependencies()` - Receives incomplete DR list\n\n3. **pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go**\n   - `destinationRule()` - Returns only consolidated DRs, not original sources\n   - `SetDestinationRules()` - Calls `mergeDestinationRule()`\n   - `consolidatedDestRules` struct - Stores only consolidated, not original, DRs\n\n4. **pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go**\n   - `checkProxyDependencies()` - Relies on complete dependency registration\n   - `ConfigAffectsProxy()` - Calls dependency check\n\n5. **pilot/pkg/bootstrap/server.go**\n   - `configHandler()` - Creates update events with original DR metadata\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Symptom:** Envoy sidecar shows stale cluster and route configuration after DestinationRule update\n   - Verified via `GET /debug/config_dump` on sidecar\n   - Pod restart picks up the change (because full recomputation happens)\n\n2. **→ xDS push was skipped** for the updated DestinationRule\n   - No CDS/RDS update was sent to the sidecar\n   - `ConfigAffectsProxy()` returned false in `proxy_dependencies.go:32-58`\n\n3. **→ Push filter rejected the update** because proxy didn't depend on the updated DR\n   - `checkProxyDependencies()` called `DependsOnConfig()` (line 64)\n   - `DependsOnConfig()` returned false (sidecar.go:538)\n\n4. **→ Updated DR's ConfigKey was not in registered dependencies**\n   - The updated DR (e.g., \"reviews-subsets\") had a ConfigKey hash not in `configDependencies`\n   - Only the first DR's ConfigKey was registered in sidecar scope initialization\n\n5. **→ Only the first DR's metadata survived consolidation**\n   - When `mergeDestinationRule()` processed the second DR (line 38-109 in destination_rule.go)\n   - It merged the second DR's specs into a copy of the first DR\n   - But did not add the second DR to `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` (line 101-104)\n   - The second DR's Name and Namespace were lost\n\n6. **→ Root cause: Merged DestinationRule loses contributor identities**\n   - `mergeDestinationRule()` consolidates multiple DRs for the same host into one\n   - The consolidated config retains the first DR's metadata\n   - Subsequent DRs' metadata is discarded after their specs are merged in\n   - No audit trail or tracking of which original DRs contributed to the consolidated config\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Fix Strategy\n\nThe root cause is the loss of identity metadata during DR consolidation. Two approaches:\n\n**Option A (Preferred): Track all contributing DRs**\n- Modify `consolidatedDestRules` to store a list of original ConfigKeys that contributed to each consolidated DR\n- When building `SidecarScope.configDependencies`, register all contributing DRs' ConfigKeys, not just the consolidated one\n- Requires changes to:\n  - `consolidatedDestRules` struct in `push_context.go` (add field like `contributingDRs map[host.Name][]ConfigKey`)\n  - `mergeDestinationRule()` in `destination_rule.go` (track which DRs were merged)\n  - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` and `ConvertToSidecarScope()` in `sidecar.go` (register all contributing DRs)\n\n**Option B (Alternative): Preserve all merged DRs separately**\n- Modify `mergeDestinationRule()` to keep all DRs (not just the consolidated one) in `p.destRules[resolvedHost]`\n- Each DR would be in the list, with their separate specs and metadata preserved\n- Requires rethinking the consolidation strategy (may have other implications for RDS/CDS generation)\n\n### Diagnostic Steps for Users\n\n1. **Check if issue is occurring:**\n   ```bash\n   # On pod with old config:\n   istioctl debug config-dump <pod> | grep -A 20 \"cluster:\"\n\n   # Check if more recent than pod restart:\n   kubectl get dr -A -o json | jq '.items[] | {name, creationTime}'\n   ```\n\n2. **Identify affected DRs:**\n   - Find all DRs for the same host: `kubectl get dr -A | grep <hostname>`\n   - Check creation times and spec differences\n   - If two or more exist for same host, they're being merged\n\n3. **Workaround (temporary):**\n   - {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01666ubGTVq4orUUVofbRxRS","type":"tool_result","content":"File created successfully at: /logs/agent/investigation.md"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"180f8079-8ed7-4c6c-b31b-59d57a0f5c38","uuid":"4778e981-90f8-4e6b-8f28-1904d181988a","tool_use_result":{"type":"create","filePath":"/logs/agent/investigation.md","content":"# Investigation Report\n\n## Summary\n\nWhen multiple DestinationRules are created for the same host, the `mergeDestinationRule()` function in `pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go` merges their specifications (subsets, traffic policies) into a single consolidated config while discarding the metadata identity of the contributing DRs. Consequently, only the first DR's ConfigKey is registered in the proxy's `SidecarScope.configDependencies`. When a contributing DR that was not preserved in the consolidated config is updated, the update event does not match any registered dependency, causing `DependsOnConfig()` to return false and the proxy push to be incorrectly skipped, leaving the Envoy sidecar with stale configuration.\n\n## Root Cause\n\n**File:** `pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go` (merging logic)\n**Function:** `mergeDestinationRule()` (lines 38-109)\n**Mechanism:** Metadata loss during consolidation\n\nWhen multiple DestinationRules target the same FQDN host:\n\n1. **First DR arrives** → added to `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` (line 107)\n2. **Second DR arrives** → merges with first:\n   - Deep copies the first DR (line 65)\n   - Merges subsets and traffic policies from second DR into the copy (lines 77-93)\n   - Updates `p.destRules[resolvedHost][0]` with the merged copy (line 66)\n   - Does **not** add the second DR as a separate entry (line 101-104: `addRuleToProcessedDestRules` is false, so the second DR is discarded)\n\n**Result:** `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` now contains only one config.Config object (the first DR, with merged specs). The second DR's identity (Name, Namespace) is permanently lost.\n\n## Evidence\n\n### 1. Merging Logic (destination_rule.go:38-109)\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig config.Config, ...) {\n    // ...line 41: If a DR already exists for this host...\n    if mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n        // ...line 65-66: Deep copy the FIRST DR, modify it in-place\n        copied := mdr.DeepCopy()\n        p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied\n\n        // ...line 77-87: Add subsets from the NEW DR to the copied FIRST DR\n        for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n            mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n        }\n\n        // ...line 91-92: Add traffic policy from NEW DR if FIRST DR doesn't have one\n        if mergedRule.TrafficPolicy == nil && rule.TrafficPolicy != nil {\n            mergedRule.TrafficPolicy = rule.TrafficPolicy\n        }\n    }\n    // ...line 101-104: If addRuleToProcessedDestRules is false, do NOT add the new DR separately\n    if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {\n        p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Key Issue:** The `destRuleConfig` (second DR) is never added to `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` when `addRuleToProcessedDestRules` is false. Its specs are merged into a copy of the first DR, but its metadata (Name, Namespace from `destRuleConfig.Name` and `destRuleConfig.Namespace`) is lost forever.\n\n### 2. Dependency Tracking in SidecarScope (sidecar.go:219-227, 410-416)\n\n**DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace (lines 219-227):**\n```go\nfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,           // Only uses the config's Name field\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace,       // Only uses the config's Namespace field\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**ConvertToSidecarScope (lines 410-416):**\n```go\nfor _, dr := range drList {\n    out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n        Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n        Name:      dr.Name,               // Only uses the config's Name field\n        Namespace: dr.Namespace,           // Only uses the config's Namespace field\n    })\n}\n```\n\n**Problem:** Both iterate over `out.destinationRules` (which comes from `ps.destinationRule()`), which returns the consolidated list from `p.destRules[hostname]`. Since only the first DR is in this list, only its ConfigKey is registered. The second DR's ConfigKey is never added to `configDependencies`.\n\n### 3. xDS Push Filter (proxy_dependencies.go:60-74)\n\n```go\nfunc checkProxyDependencies(proxy *model.Proxy, config model.ConfigKey) bool {\n    switch proxy.Type {\n    case model.SidecarProxy:\n        if proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {  // Line 64\n            return true\n        } else if proxy.PrevSidecarScope != nil && proxy.PrevSidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n    return false\n}\n```\n\n**DependsOnConfig (sidecar.go:523-540):**\n```go\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) DependsOnConfig(config ConfigKey) bool {\n    // ... check for cluster-scoped configs ...\n\n    // Line 538: Check if this config's hash is in registered dependencies\n    _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n    return exists\n}\n```\n\n**Failure:** When an update event for the second DR (reviews-subsets) arrives, it creates a ConfigKey with Name=\"reviews-subsets\" and Namespace=\"default\". The hash of this key is looked up in `configDependencies`. Since only the first DR's key is registered, the lookup fails and `DependsOnConfig()` returns false. The proxy is not pushed.\n\n### 4. Config Update Event Handler (bootstrap/server.go:881-904)\n\n```go\nconfigHandler := func(prev config.Config, curr config.Config, event model.Event) {\n    pushReq := &model.PushRequest{\n        Full: true,\n        ConfigsUpdated: map[model.ConfigKey]struct{}{{\n            Kind:      curr.GroupVersionKind,       // DestinationRule\n            Name:      curr.Name,                   // reviews-subsets (when updated)\n            Namespace: curr.Namespace,               // default\n        }: {}},\n        Reason: []model.TriggerReason{model.ConfigUpdate},\n    }\n    s.XDSServer.ConfigUpdate(pushReq)\n}\n```\n\n**Result:** When `reviews-subsets` is updated, the event handler creates a PushRequest with ConfigKey{Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\"}. However, the proxy's `SidecarScope.configDependencies` only contains the hash of ConfigKey{Name: \"reviews-traffic-policy\", Namespace: \"default\"}. The push filtering rejects the update as not affecting this proxy.\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go**\n   - `mergeDestinationRule()` - Merges multiple DRs but discards metadata identity\n\n2. **pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go**\n   - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` - Registers only DRs present in consolidated list\n   - `ConvertToSidecarScope()` - Same limitation\n   - `AddConfigDependencies()` - Receives incomplete DR list\n\n3. **pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go**\n   - `destinationRule()` - Returns only consolidated DRs, not original sources\n   - `SetDestinationRules()` - Calls `mergeDestinationRule()`\n   - `consolidatedDestRules` struct - Stores only consolidated, not original, DRs\n\n4. **pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go**\n   - `checkProxyDependencies()` - Relies on complete dependency registration\n   - `ConfigAffectsProxy()` - Calls dependency check\n\n5. **pilot/pkg/bootstrap/server.go**\n   - `configHandler()` - Creates update events with original DR metadata\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Symptom:** Envoy sidecar shows stale cluster and route configuration after DestinationRule update\n   - Verified via `GET /debug/config_dump` on sidecar\n   - Pod restart picks up the change (because full recomputation happens)\n\n2. **→ xDS push was skipped** for the updated DestinationRule\n   - No CDS/RDS update was sent to the sidecar\n   - `ConfigAffectsProxy()` returned false in `proxy_dependencies.go:32-58`\n\n3. **→ Push filter rejected the update** because proxy didn't depend on the updated DR\n   - `checkProxyDependencies()` called `DependsOnConfig()` (line 64)\n   - `DependsOnConfig()` returned false (sidecar.go:538)\n\n4. **→ Updated DR's ConfigKey was not in registered dependencies**\n   - The updated DR (e.g., \"reviews-subsets\") had a ConfigKey hash not in `configDependencies`\n   - Only the first DR's ConfigKey was registered in sidecar scope initialization\n\n5. **→ Only the first DR's metadata survived consolidation**\n   - When `mergeDestinationRule()` processed the second DR (line 38-109 in destination_rule.go)\n   - It merged the second DR's specs into a copy of the first DR\n   - But did not add the second DR to `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` (line 101-104)\n   - The second DR's Name and Namespace were lost\n\n6. **→ Root cause: Merged DestinationRule loses contributor identities**\n   - `mergeDestinationRule()` consolidates multiple DRs for the same host into one\n   - The consolidated config retains the first DR's metadata\n   - Subsequent DRs' metadata is discarded after their specs are merged in\n   - No audit trail or tracking of which original DRs contributed to the consolidated config\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Fix Strategy\n\nThe root cause is the loss of identity metadata during DR consolidation. Two approaches:\n\n**Option A (Preferred): Track all contributing DRs**\n- Modify `consolidatedDestRules` to store a list of original ConfigKeys that contributed to each consolidated DR\n- When building `SidecarScope.configDependencies`, register all contributing DRs' ConfigKeys, not just the consolidated one\n- Requires changes to:\n  - `consolidatedDestRules` struct in `push_context.go` (add field like `contributingDRs map[host.Name][]ConfigKey`)\n  - `mergeDestinationRule()` in `destination_rule.go` (track which DRs were merged)\n  - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` and `ConvertToSidecarScope()` in `sidecar.go` (register all contributing DRs)\n\n**Option B (Alternative): Preserve all merged DRs separately**\n- Modify `mergeDestinationRule()` to keep all DRs (not just the consolidated one) in `p.destRules[resolvedHost]`\n- Each DR would be in the list, with their separate specs and metadata preserved\n- Requires rethinking the consolidation strategy (may have other implications for RDS/CDS generation)\n\n### Diagnostic Steps for Users\n\n1. **Check if issue is occurring:**\n   ```bash\n   # On pod with old config:\n   istioctl debug config-dump <pod> | grep -A 20 \"cluster:\"\n\n   # Check if more recent than pod restart:\n   kubectl get dr -A -o json | jq '.items[] | {name, creationTime}'\n   ```\n\n2. **Identify affected DRs:**\n   - Find all DRs for the same host: `kubectl get dr -A | grep <hostname>`\n   - Check creation times and spec differences\n   - If two or more exist for same host, they're being merged\n\n3. **Workaround (temporary):**\n   - Combine conflicting DRs into a single DestinationRule with all subsets and policies\n   - Delete the redundant DRs\n   - Verify pod picks up changes without restart\n\n4. **Verify fix:**\n   - After fix, update one of multiple DRs for same host\n   - Monitor sidecar logs: `kubectl logs <pod> -c istio-proxy | grep updated`\n   - Check `config_dump` for fresh timestamps\n   - No pod restart should be needed\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
